[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentified this as a wild address read with a scariness score of [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Overview[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzing campaign targeting the `handler_bat.vis` fuzzer detected a memory [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafety violation in Wireshark's packet dissection code. The crash manifests as an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer SEGV error when attempting to read from an invalid memory address [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x202020a0030c28[0m[39m`. The issue is triggered when processing a specifically crafted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest case through the BAT.VIS protocol dissector.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a memory safety vulnerability, specifically:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **SEGV [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSegmentation Fault[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** on an unknown address[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Wild Address Read** - attempting to read from an unmapped or invalid memory [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocation[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error occurs during a memory access operation within format string processing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Technical Details[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals the following execution flow:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The crash originates in `dissect_bat_vis_v24` function at [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-bat.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m705[0m[39m`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The immediate cause is within the `__fprintf_chk` function, specifically during [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat string processing[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The call chain shows: `dissect_bat_vis_v24` → `__fprintf_chk` → `vfprintf` → [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`printf_common` → `QuickCheckForUnpoisonedRegion`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The error occurs when AddressSanitizer's memory access checking detects an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempt to read from an invalid address[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Input Analysis[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer-generated input that triggers the crash contains:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple format string specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%x`, `%n`, `%s`[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Repeated patterns of [0m[32m'A'[0m[39m characters [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x41[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The presence of `%n` format specifiers is particularly noteworthy as they can [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite to memory locations[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The input appears to be attempting to exploit format string vulnerabilities[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have identified the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause and necessary fixes:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash is caused by a **format string vulnerability** in `[0m[1;35mdissect_bat_vis_v24[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `d_output_buffer` contains user-controlled packet data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vis_packeth_raw_data`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that includes format specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%x`, `%n`, `%s`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. When [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed directly as the format string argument to `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, these specifiers are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpreted, causing memory access violations and crashes.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Findings[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Format String Vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m: User data copied into `d_output_buffer` via `[0m[1;35msnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m: `d_output_buffer` used directly as format string in `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzer input with `%x`, `%n`, `%s` triggers SEGV when fprintf interprets them[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Debug Code in Production**: The entire raw_data feature [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m646[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m648[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m653[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is debug code that:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Violates Wireshark coding standards [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfprintf forbidden in dissectors[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduces security vulnerabilities[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Serves no legitimate dissection purpose[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Is not part of protocol specification[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Is not present in v22 or v23 implementations[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Multiple Implementation Errors**:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Missing null termination of `vis_packeth_raw_data` buffer[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Incorrect offset handling: `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset++, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` only increments [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, not [0m[1;36m4[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Wrong encoding parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m instead of ENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Offset corruption causing wrong data added to protocol tree[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **V24 Protocol Analysis**: V24 uses `struct vis_packet_v23` and [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`VIS_PACKET_V23_SIZE`, indicating the protocol format is identical to v23. The [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraw_data feature is an unauthorized addition.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Comparison with Working Implementations[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**V23 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCorrect Pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Clean parsing from fixed offsets[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No fprintf/debug output[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Proper offset tracking[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Standard proto_tree_add_* functions only[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**V24 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBroken[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Starts at offset [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m instead of [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reads undefined raw_data field[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses vulnerable fprintf[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Confused offset tracking[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove All Raw_Data Related Code[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFrom `[0m[1;35mdissect_bat_vis_v24[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, remove the following:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Variable declarations** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m646[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m648[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   int [0m[33mvis_packeth_raw_data_size[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   char vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   char d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Buffer initialization** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m653[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Raw_data reading** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   vis_packeth_raw_data_size = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset++, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   offset += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size > [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   for [0m[1;39m([0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < vis_packeth_raw_data_size; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       offset++;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Debug output** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m687[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Vulnerable fprintf** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Complete Corrected Implementation[0m                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `[0m[1;35mdissect_bat_vis_v24[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function should mirror the v23 implementation exactly:[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_max_tq_v23, tvb, offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m*offset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;*[0m[35m/[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Calculate offset even when we got no tree *[0m[35m/[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    offset = VIS_PACKET_V23_SIZE;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtap_queue_packet[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_tap, pinfo, vis_packeth[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    length_remaining = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < length_remaining; i += VIS_PACKET_V23_DATA_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        next_tvb = [0m[1;35mtvb_new_subset_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, VIS_PACKET_V23_DATA_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mhave_tap_listener[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_follow_tap[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mtap_queue_packet[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_follow_tap, pinfo, next_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mdissect_vis_entry_v23[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext_tvb, pinfo, tree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        offset += VIS_PACKET_V23_DATA_SIZE;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    length_remaining = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength_remaining > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        next_tvb = [0m[1;35mtvb_new_subset_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mhave_tap_listener[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_follow_tap[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mtap_queue_packet[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_follow_tap, pinfo, next_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mcall_data_dissector[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext_tvb, pinfo, tree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Root Cause**: Removes the format string vulnerability completely by[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoving fprintf and all user-controlled format string usage[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Established Pattern**: Makes v24 identical to the working v23 [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation, ensuring consistency and correctness[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Protocol Compatibility**: The fix assumes v24 protocol format is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical to v23 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mevidenced by using `struct vis_packet_v23`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is the safest [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massumption[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: The remaining data processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m707[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m736[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged and continues to work correctly[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Complies with Wireshark Standards**: Removes forbidden fprintf calls and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollows proper dissector patterns[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Minimal Risk**: Simply removes broken debug code without changing core [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissection logic[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All proto_tree_add_* calls remain the same[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;35mtap_queue_packet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls unchanged[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Data entry processing loop unchanged[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only removes problematic debug code that was never part of the protocol [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecification[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Addresses Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **SEGV Crash**: Fixed by removing fprintf with user-controlled format string[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Format String Vulnerability**: Eliminated by removing all format string [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing of user data[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Safety**: Removed buffer overflow risks from raw_data reading[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Coding Standards**: Removes forbidden fprintf usage[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m Expected**:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Raw_data was only used for debug fprintf output[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No other code references these variables[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No header fields defined for raw_data[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- v22 and v23 work correctly without this code[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removing debug code cannot break existing functionality[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Considered and Rejected[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative Fix**: Replace `[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rejected Because**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- fprintf still violates Wireshark coding standards[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still has missing null termination issues[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still has incorrect offset handling[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still adds no value to dissection[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Proper fix is to remove the debug code entirely[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Conclusion[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy completely eliminates the format string vulnerability by removing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall debug code that was improperly added to the v24 handler. The resulting [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation matches the proven-correct v23 pattern, ensuring security, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectness, and maintainability. The fix is minimal, focused, and carries no risk [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof breaking existing functionality since it only removes code that was never part [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the legitimate dissector implementation.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
